[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected in the Apache [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika CSV/Text parser. The fuzzer identified that the parser attempts to make an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound connection to an external domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input data. This vulnerability is classified as a medium severity [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue, as it could potentially lead to exfiltration of sensitive data or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munauthorized access to internal services.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** vulnerability, where an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication can be manipulated to make unauthorized HTTP/HTTPS requests to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary destinations based on untrusted user-supplied data.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Observed Behavior[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer detected an attempted HTTPS connection to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m` originating [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the `TextAndCSVParser` component of Apache Tika. The stack trace reveals the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing execution flow:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with test data[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This calls `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParserFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which invokes the Tika parser[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method processes the input[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. During cell processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the parser calls `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` attempts to open an HTTPS connection to an external URL[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The Java networking stack establishes an SSL socket connection to the external [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdestination[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe security sanitizer intercepted this connection attempt at the socket level [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the actual network request was completed, triggering the security exception.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Input-Driven URL Resolution**: The parser appears to interpret certain cell [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent as URLs and automatically attempts to fetch/process them without proper [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation or sanitization of the destination.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lack of URL Validation**: There is no apparent allowlist or validation [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism preventing connections to arbitrary external or internal destinations [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbased on cell content.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Automatic URL Processing**: The `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in `TextAndCSVParser` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mautomatically processes URLs found in CSV cells, making the parser susceptible to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF attacks when handling untrusted input files.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVParser**:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m278[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - understand what triggers URL processing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand how URLs are extracted[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m261[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - examine how cells are analyzed and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen URL processing is invoked[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - review the overall parsing logic and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration options[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Configuration and Settings**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Investigate whether there are configuration options to disable automatic URL [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetching[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Determine if there are any existing security controls or allowlist mechanisms [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat are not being applied[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **URL Detection Logic**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Examine how the parser identifies content as URLs within CSV cells[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Understand what URL schemes are supported [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP, HTTPS, FILE, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Similar Patterns**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if other Tika parsers have similar URL processing behavior[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review if this pattern exists in other cell processing logic within the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis vulnerability poses a significant security risk as it allows attackers to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcraft malicious CSV files that could trigger requests to internal services, cloud [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata endpoints, or exfiltrate data to external domains when processed by the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy for SSRF Vulnerability in TextAndCSVParser[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability occurs in the `TextAndCSVParser` class when processing CSV [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles containing Excel-style `=[0m[1;35mHYPERLINK[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` formulas. The vulnerable code flow is:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Detection**: The parser detects HYPERLINK formulas using regex pattern [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **HTML Generation**: Creates an HTML anchor tag with the extracted URL [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Automatic URL Fetching**: **Unconditionally calls `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`** at line [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m261[0m[39m, which:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Opens a URL connection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m276[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fetches content via `[0m[1;35mconnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m278[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parses the fetched content as an embedded document [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m279[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Issue**: The URL connection is established **before** any security [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can be applied, and there's no configuration [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moption to disable this behavior. This allows malicious CSV files to trigger [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequests to arbitrary external or internal destinations.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImplement a **secure-by-default** configuration flag to control URL fetching [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior, following the established pattern used in `PDFParserConfig` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`extractInlineImages`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Extend TextAndCSVConfig Class[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd a new boolean field to control URL fetching behavior:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodule/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/TextAndCSVConfig.java`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: After the existing delimiter map fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m42[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add private field: `private boolean fetchHyperlinks = false;`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - **Default value MUST be `false`** to prevent SSRF by default[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - This is a security-critical default following the principle of [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure-by-default[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add getter method:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```java[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  public boolean [0m[1;35misFetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return fetchHyperlinks;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add setter method:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```java[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  public void [0m[1;35msetFetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean fetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      this.fetchHyperlinks = fetchHyperlinks;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Centralizes configuration in the dedicated config class[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains consistency with existing delimiter configuration pattern[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allows serialization and persistence of configuration[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Configuration Delegation in TextAndCSVParser[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodule/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/TextAndCSVParser.java`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix Strategy is Optimal[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Security Benefits[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Secure by Default**: URL fetching is disabled by default, preventing SSRF [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Requires explicit opt-in to enable risky behavior[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible Security**: Existing deployments automatically get the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity fix[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Zero-Day Protection**: Protects against unknown CSV files with malicious [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhyperlinks[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **HTML Generation Preserved**: Anchor tags are still created from HYPERLINK [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformulas[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **CSV Parsing Intact**: Core CSV/TSV parsing logic remains unchanged[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Text Extraction Maintained**: Plain text cells continue to work identically[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Existing Tests Pass**: Tests verifying anchor tag creation continue to work[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Pattern Detection Unchanged**: HYPERLINK regex pattern matching is preserved[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Follows Tika Patterns[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistent with PDFParser**: Mirrors the `extractInlineImages` configuration [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Standard @Field Usage**: Uses Tika's configuration annotation framework[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Config Class Pattern**: Extends the existing TextAndCSVConfig appropriately[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **XML Configurable**: Supports Tika's XML configuration files[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **ParseContext Override**: Allows per-invocation configuration via ParseContext[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Flexibility[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Multiple Configuration Methods**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Programmatic: `[0m[1;35mparser.setFetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - XML: `<param [0m[33mname[0m[39m=[0m[32m"fetchHyperlinks"[0m[39m [0m[33mtype[0m[39m=[0m[32m"bool"[0m[39m>true<[0m[35m/[0m[95mparam[0m[39m>`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ParseContext: Per-invocation override[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Granular Control**: Can be enabled for specific parsing operations only[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Future Extensibility**: Could be enhanced with URL allowlists/blocklists later[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Addressing Potential Side Effects[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Impact on Existing Deployments[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Positive**: Automatically prevents SSRF vulnerabilities in existing systems[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Minimal Disruption**: Only affects CSV files with HYPERLINK formulas that were [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing fetched[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Most Users Unaffected**: URL fetching is a niche feature most users don't rely [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Migration Path for Users Who Need URL Fetching[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUsers who explicitly need URL fetching behavior can re-enable it via:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XML Configuration**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```xml[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<parser [0m[33mclass[0m[39m=[0m[32m"org[0m[32m.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVParser"[0m[39m>[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    <params>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <param [0m[33mname[0m[39m=[0m[32m"fetchHyperlinks"[0m[39m [0m[33mtype[0m[39m=[0m[32m"bool"[0m[39m>true<[0m[35m/[0m[95mparam[0m[39m>[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    <[0m[35m/[0m[95mparams[0m[39m>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mparser[0m[39m>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Programmatic Configuration**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTextAndCSVParser parser = new [0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparser.setFetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Per-Invocation Configuration**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTextAndCSVConfig config = new [0m[1;35mTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mconfig.setFetchHyperlinks[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParseContext context = new [0m[1;35mParseContext[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcontext.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, config[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstream, handler, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Compatibility Considerations[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No API Changes**: No method signatures are modified[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No Removed Functionality**: URL fetching capability is preserved [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjust opt-in[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No Breaking Changes**: Tests and existing code continue to work[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No External Dependencies**: No new libraries required[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Check [0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Before Opening Connection[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would require restructuring [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to set metadata before connection[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still requires users to set up DocumentSelector to prevent SSRF[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Not secure by default - users must actively configure filtering[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More complex implementation with more potential failure points[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Call Entirely[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes functionality that some users may legitimately use[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Too aggressive - eliminates a feature rather than securing it[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No migration path for users who need the feature[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Not aligned with Tika's philosophy of comprehensive document processing[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add URL Allowlist/Blocklist[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More complex to implement and configure correctly[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still vulnerable if allowlist is misconfigured[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Not secure by default unless blocklist includes everything [0m[1;39m([0m[39mequivalent to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Can be added as a future enhancement on top of this fix[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Alternative [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Modify [0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Check in EmbeddedDocumentExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Requires changes to core Tika classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEmbeddedDocumentExtractor[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Broader impact beyond TextAndCSVParser[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Connection is already opened before [0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m could be checked[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would need to refactor [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m significantly anyway[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing Strategy[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Existing Tests[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify existing tests continue to pass without modifications[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Specifically verify `[0m[1;35mtestHyperlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` passes [0m[1;39m([0m[39manchor tag creation[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### New Tests Needed[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Test default behavior** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL fetching disabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parse CSV with HYPERLINK formula[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify anchor tag is created[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify no network connection is attempted [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmock URLConnection[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Test enabled behavior** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL fetching enabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Set [0m[33mfetchHyperlinks[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parse CSV with HYPERLINK formula[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify URL content is fetched and parsed[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test configuration methods**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test @Field annotation via XML config[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test programmatic setter[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test ParseContext override[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Documentation Updates Needed[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **JavaDoc Updates**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add security warning to [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document the configuration option with security implications[0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Explain migration path for users needing URL fetching[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Emphasize secure-by-default nature[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Security Advisory** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif applicable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document the SSRF vulnerability[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy provides a **secure-by-default** solution that:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Eliminates the SSRF vulnerability** by disabling URL fetching by default[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Preserves all existing functionality** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTML anchor tag generation[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Maintains backward compatibility** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexisting tests pass[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Follows established Tika patterns** [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimilar to PDFParser configuration[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Provides flexibility** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmultiple configuration methods[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Requires minimal code changes** [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m files modified[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **Has clear migration path** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mopt-in for users who need URL fetching[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **No external dependencies** [0m[1;39m([0m[39muses existing Tika framework[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **No modifications to fuzzing harness** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfix is in source code only[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ **No modifications to test infrastructure** [0m[1;39m([0m[39muses existing test framework[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe implementation is straightforward, secure, and aligned with Tika's architecture[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand security principles.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
